Tuddington : which gaue me satisfaction of your being well , so fare on
your journey : which ascurance of your health is the beest nwes <P_2> I
can heare , except that of your comeing home . HARLEY,2.002.12

RECIPIENT:EDWARD_HARLEY:MALE:SON:1624:15
LETTER:HARLEY_063:E2:1639:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
Ned Harley - By my last I acquainted you of my purpose to send horses
for you and your worthy tutor , if your logicke or rethoricke can
prevayle with hym to honoure you heere with his presence , and my
resolution hereby <paren> God will'ge </paren> to send them that they
may arrive with you on the 11th of the next month . HARLEY,212.063.1755

RECIPIENT:EDWARD_HARLEY:MALE:SON:1624:15
LETTER:HARLEY_063:E2:1639:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
But if the tutors affaires stand calculated for an other meridian in
the verticole point of this yeare , then let this berer , in his
returne from London , bring mee a cleere understonding of it ,
HARLEY,212.063.1756

LETTER:HARLEY_068:E3:1654:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
Sir , if our Lord God see it good to permitt Satan to discover his
malice , be pleased to consider that your age and weakness , which
encourage Satan to assault you : they doe much more assure you of
victory , because all the retrenchments from your own ability to resist
, doe place you more closely and imediately under the secure protection
of the Lord of Hosts , who I doubt not will graciously avenge you of
your spirituall adversary ; will make His candle shine upon your head ,
and having sanctified all His dispensatins towards you , will fully
assure you , that having given you His son , how shall He not with Him
also freely give you all things . HARLEY,217.068.1812

granted by your society to my wifes mother , the Lady Button , and by
her death accrewing to us , wee desire in Gods fear , so far as lies in
us , to restore that portion of the Lords to the seruice of the Lord .

but we hope God will inclin the hearts of so worthy a school of the

years . In order to which we are willing to resign our leas upon these
terms ,- viz. That you wil promis under your hands to joyn your best
endevors with ours , that assoon as may be , by act of Parlement , the
profits of the rectory of Folden surmounting your rent reserued upon
our leas , may be vnited to the vicarag , and settled for ever upon the
incumbent minister at Folden ; that until this vnion be effected ,
according to law , you will renew the leas for twenty - and one years
future , either-5 to myself or some other person of responsible estat
and integrity , only in trust and for the use and benefit of the
minister of Folden for the time being , which leassee shal also giv
bond of lb. penalty not to conuert the profits aforsaid to any other
use then is expressed . HARLEY,237.073.1894
